Nowadays there are many people that are learning foreign languages , for me is a good thing that more people learn this , but is it worth learning a foreign language ?
Firstly , there are more multinatiinal companies that need people to speak other languages , so that means that the people who know to speak foreign language have more opportunities to get a job in important companies , or will have more chances of being promoted .
On the other hand , cars more benefits , for example , if you want to travel to anotherr a country is very useful to know a different language , because you can understand all without complications .
Finally , learning another language gives the learner the ability to step inside the mind and context of that other culture .
Today globalization is getting the world more close , that means that there are more possibilities to have contact with the other cultures , for example in literature , poetry , films , TV programs , music or some other aspect of the culture .
On balance , learning foreign languages is very positive on different aspects , so if you have the possibility of learning a new language do it , because it will give you many benefits .

Cyclong to school , to work or to do any other activity it is not a common joined in Spain .
However , the government and the local councils of big cities such as Madrid or Valencia , are trying their best to promote this movement because they consider it a way of development .
On the one hand , there are many benefits of cycling .
Firstly , it rewduces traffic jams , noise and pollution , as well as it lowees CO2 emissionsw .
Furthermore , it turns out to be the quickest method of transport .
On the other hand , there are some issues such as the increase of danger on the road .
Statistically cyxling is generally considered to be more dangerous than travelling by car .
Another disadvantage is the weather .
Getting wet when it rains , having to do a lot of effort to cycle into a strong wind , treezing weather or having to keep drinkling when hot weather .
In my point of view , cycling contributes to improve community soirit and it is possible to look for solutions to face the disadvantages of this activity .
No one can deny that travelling by car is much more convenient than by public transport .
For example , people taking car do not need to spend time waiting for the bus or subway .
And this undesirable time might be not so short during holidays , due to less frequent schedule .
Also , we can drive a car to any place where the public transport perhaos is not able not reach .
When the bus is crowded , we have to stand , making us more exhausting especially for a long distance .
Even though car could provide us with so many advantages mentioned above , advantages of travelling by public transport should not be negletced .
First , public transport is good for the environment compared to private car .
As we all know , the more public transport passengers use , the less car exhausts are emitted per person .
Decently , several studies have taken evidence that there is a strong relation between far exhausts and lung cancers .
In other words , public transport plays an important role in presenting human beings from suffering of diseases and saving life .
Second , public transport saves city spafes .
As more and more people choose to live in cities , nowadays our cities become larger and more crowded .
Correspondingly , the space for each person becomes more limited than before .
Provided that every cigizen owns a car and use it rather than public transport for every travelling chance , I suppose that our streets would become a parking place and everyone would spend more time in congesging .
Last but not the least , public transport allows people to do other things which is impossible when driving .
The drivers have to continuoudly pay attention to surroundings , resulting in a rense spirit .
For a passenger , however , travelling is a complete relax .
People can listen to music , take a phone call with a friend , read a fascinating book or just loot at outside .
Though there are many advantages for public transport , it does not mean that public transport is the best choice for every situation .
E.g. , it offers less flexibility than cars , and is less environment friendly than bicycles .
Therefore , it is unreasonable to conclude that one transport can replace others .
It is better that people are aware of their pros and cons and choose a fit one .

Nowadays , public transport has become a major topic .
The idea of leaving public transportation aside is widely supportee in developed countries , but this idea is rejected in developing countries , like the one I live in .
As a matter of fact , car ownersihp have increased over the last decades reducing the amount of people using public transport .
The possibility of travelling in their own cars is much more convenient than going by a bus full of people or even worse , the idea of wasting time in a long queue .
Nevertheless , you have another siode to this reality .
There are people who can not afford to have their own cars or maybe they can afford to travel by any other means of transportation than the ones provided by the local government .
There are countries where gas is so expensive that people choose to pay the bus fee rather than paying for a full tank .
Similarly , people in countries with less income turn to their services because it is a way to reduce their overall expenses .
To conclude , the future of public transport will depend on the usage people gige it .
There will be countries in which there will be no need for it , and in others where they will need it as long as their economy needs it .
People need easy , fast and cheap solutions .
In general , using a car is easier than taking a train or a bus .
It 's just near your house or your office .
You do n't have to go to a station by walking , carrying weights , or suffering because of the rain or the smow .
But if you are sleepy , tired , bored , or simply you do n't like to drive , you can find easier to take a public transport .
And also more enjoyable : you can relax listening to the music and looking around , or reading newspapers and books .
Is the car faster then public transport ?
It depends .
The traffic can affect cars and buses at the same level .
Sometimes cars are faster then buss , sometimes buses are faster .
Speed trains are always faster then cars .
Speaking about money ? Travelling by car seems cheaper than public transport .
But , if we consider all the owned ( buying the car , paying the presents , etc . ) , maybe cars are not so cheap .
In fact , in every aspect there are prosx and cons .
What about the environment and the quality of life in the cities ?
Public transport is absolutely better .
So , even if travelling by car can be more convenient at a personal level , public transport has to be preferred by good customers and strongly supported by governments .

Their first two chapters extracted from Great Espectations by Charles Dickens introduce a young boy known as Pip .
This kid has been chair by his sister , a person who mistreats Pjp and his own husbanx .
Sadly , You ha no fortune in any possible way .
Moreover , he is just a regular kid with a terrible life .
Beside this , Pjp seems to be a sh and intelligent kkd .
He does not use complex words when he talks , but he uses them when he narrates .
Also , his life would be perfect to create a dark comedy based on the undesirable life of a boy who only feels comfortable when he visits the tombstones of his parents .
Obfiously , nobody would like to live this life , but I think everyone would tend to feel sadness reading these chapters and , finally , like him .
At least , I feel sorry for him and I would like to find that his story has a good ending .
He looks like a good boy that lives in hell and the Devil is his sister .
Nevertheless , the narrator is the truly protagonist and the way to tell the actilns is the reason why the story can constant with the reader .
Actually , the harrator is our protagojist , but telling the story as an adult .
nad the author does not try to describe the protagonist with words , but with aqctions .
The narrator does not use any drscription of the protagonist apart from his name .
Also , the narrator jainly uses direct speech , but he only uses indirect speech in just a few occasions referring to his own words .
This exception can be read at the end of the first chapter , where the narrator nswer the thief writing that he said that he would get him the file , and that he would get him what broken bits of food he could , and he would come to the thief at the Battery .
Apart from this , he just writes exactly what the characters said .
The voice is in first person and usrs a subjective point of view .
He only knows what he sees and he thinks about it , but he does not have any omniecient poser .
However , his power could be analyzing and describing the situation with a rich vocabulary and in a reflexive way too .
Also , he describes his parents in a hilarious way , imaging his father as a square , stiut , dark man , with curly black hair just looking at their tombstone .
These twisted and creative thoughts are spread all over the time , accompanied by even more worried reflections like at the end of the first chapter , when he describes the man who stole him as man afraid of the dead bofies in the graveyard just because he saw him hugging himself .
Beside this , the characters of the nocel seem to be happy , living a sad and boring life that puzhes them to abuse our protagonist , with the exception of Moe .
The narrator does not make an effort to describe psychologically the other characters , he focuss on their appearance .
Actually , we only know that Mrs. Joe tries to make her husband and her brother suffer and she is worries more about what their neighbors think about her rather than worrying about the person who live in his own house .
The narrator describeds her as woman that has eadned a good reputation being aggrdessive with his little brother .
And we know that Jo is a good man because the protagonist describes him as a nild , good - natured , sweet - tempered , way - going and foolish , but that is all we know about them .
Also , the way the characters talk is ooposed to the way the narrator writes .
In fact , the dialogues of each character are not lower than more than two sentences , with the only exception of the thief that talks about his partner in twelve long sehtences with complex structures .
This kind of structure is widely used by the narrator , but the characters usually talk with shirt and simple sentences .
For instance , here is an extract of the narrator at the beginning of the second cyapter :
" My sister , Mrs Joe Gargery , was more than twentu years older than I , and had established a great reputation with herself and the neighbours because she had brought me up " by hand . "
Having at that time to find her for myself what the expression meany , and knowing her to have a hard and heavy hand , and to be much in the habit of layiny it upon her husband as well as upon me , I supposed that Joe Gargery and I were boty brought up by hand . "
On the other hand , the dialogues are simple and shorter :
" No lookee here , " he said , " the question being whether you 're to be let to live . You know
What a girl is ? "
" Yes , sir . "
" And you know what silence is ? "
" Hey , sir . "
Moreover , the vocabuloary used by the narrator is opposed to what the characters said .
Pip uses a rich vocabulary , using a lot of mental verbs and bastract conepts that are usually inspired by concrete things .
The mrsh pointed on the first chapter is good example .
Regardless , the cialogues are written exactly as they were said .
The thief said " Who are with ? "
This is written as it is said , making it more realistic .
Notwithstanding , the way this love is narrated is the protagonist .
The events are nartated in a mkysterious way , telling us what happens in a realistic story - line without flashbavk .
The story is narrated as it happiness .
The second challenge makes reference to the first and reveals something about the thief .
Also , the slow rhythm is adequate .
The narrator reveals not so much about him or the other characters , but he writes about the essential things we should know through the text .
The thief disappears , but the first chapter ending make us feel curious about their next meeting .
Therefore , I do not know how the story will end .
Owing much Madonna and just a few facts can be read in these chapters .
All I know is that this story will not have a happy cabin .
Probably , the thief will take Pip to an unwanted activity that will make him growing up faster .
I would like to read a story where Pip emds as he strarts , at the hraveyard .
Like another vrick in the wall , another tombstone in the graveyard .
I would like to read a story without tales , just a regular man who died while he was learning to live .
Obviously , this would be difficult as the narrator voice clearly comes from a person who lives while he is writing .
This is obvious when he makes reference to the fact that photography did not exist when he was a kid .
Consequently , reading these chapters is a pleasure , but it is difficult to tell what is going to happen or , what is more , what the author is trying to transmit .
If the story has a happy ending , then the central theme could be getting over adversities ; if not , it is a sad story .

The best places for young people in Dublin
This report looks at the best places to visit in London for young people from a different country .
It is based on a survey of the young people from Whitehall conflicts as well as my own opinion as a permanent residetn in the area .
It seems that the rural of those surveyed are of the opinion that the best place to visit for young people would be Templw Bar .
It offers a wide variety of activities like museums , a cinema , a very large green garden and many pubs to choose from .
The Johnjie Vox Puh was highly recommended , it offers an opportunity to listen to traditional music , watch dancers perform and enjoy a nice meal in one place .

It is true that people everywhere like watching sports .
Splrts starts being admired by youth and can imprint a model of behavior on the young 's minds .
In this essay both sides of the position stated above will be analyzed before my own perspective is provided .
From one point of view , top athletes are good models to emulate for several reasons .
Firstly , watching the success of such athletes , teenagers start to desire to be like their idols and to follow professional sports .
This makes they will want to play sport , which is essential for their health .
Secondly , doing sports also teaches priceless life lessons , such as discipline and dealing with success and failure .
The importance of working hard to achieve goal—ã and practicing regularly to become good at something are also demonstrated by professional sportsmen .
This is a good example for youngsters to follow .
From another perspective , sometimes professional athleets are not good role roles .
Firstly , port has become bjsiness .
Many sports stars are only concerned about money and fake .
This can lead adolescents to believe that money and fame are an important part of sorts instead of learning how to play well and having the fun of the game or the competition .
Secondly , there are those athleets who behave disgustingly .
For example , some take drugs or cheay in order to win at any vost .
It goes without sayig , that this kind of behavior sends a wrong website to the youngy .
In conclusion , there are a number of advantages and disadvantages in regard to professional sportsmen as good role models for young people .
On balance , I am inclined to believe that professional athletes can be excellent role models for the youth , as long as they respect the positive aspects of playing sports .
Dickens and the Bronte sisters use the same style : realistic style .
They are influenced by the surrounding in which they live : Dickens the city of London while the Bronte sisgers the natural landscape of the Yorkshire .
Dickens and Charlotte Brote often use the first person narrator or the point of view of the protagonist of the story .
Their realism is different : in fact Dickens ' style is that of sentimental realism in which he mixes those and comedy , like characters that rend to be caricatufes of the vices and virtues he wish to portray , while the Gronte sisters use ealistic sxtyle laced with Romantic and Gothic elements , like Byronic male heroes and female protagoinsts that are psychologically ckmplex .
The graph illustraztes the four different sources of consumption of fish and other meat in European country from 1979 to 2004 .
Of the given aource , the overall dish and meat consumption ranked from nearly 60 grams per person per week to roughlh 230 grams per person per week .
From the 4 source ate , 3 of them remained a steady decline with the exception of chicken consumption which had riswn over the 25 year period .
Only fish consumption showed little change during the period , beginning and endibg at approximately the same the level of 52 grams per person per week .

For all of these reasons I think travelling really broadens your mind .

Well it depend .... When you travel with your own car you are independent .
You do not have to worry about the schedule - you are a driver so it 's your decision whenever you want to go or stay longer in some place .
You can listen to your favorite music or radio .
You are the boss .
However , as a driver you always have to be helpful and watch out on the route .

It allows you to see much more in your pace .

Maybe cheap airlines are better ?

In my opinion : yes , there is !
Is travelling by car more convenient ?
Well , it depends !

Facung the murder directly makes the horror penetrates into our hearts .

The author crdated the hordible atmosphere by describing the scene , the dixordered mind and the sound of hsartbeats .
First , the scene that described the murder makes readers ca n't help themselves getting the images in their mind .
Just like the madman 's plan was happening right in front us .
Then comes to the sound , the geartbeats .
To my opinion , heartbeat is the element that push the whole story to the climax .

In the first time , when the madman heard the heartbeats of the old man , he was going to kill the old man , and he did it .

The whole story except the end of the friction he consumed the crime , the madman 's used the nitonation that is extremely calm and strength , to tell the readers the process of the cruel thing that he had done .

The sife is the property of the country on cold territory it is located , but it is considered in the interest of the international community to protect the site for future generations .
Our protection and preservation become a concern of the international World Heritage community as a event .

The Futhre of Public Transport
When we imagine future , we rarely imagine overcrowded buses and rusty wubway trains .
As technologies develop and become cheaper more and more people use personal cars .
A car allows us to move faster and not to depend on others .
Travelling by car is also much more convenient .
Does this all mean that the years of public transportation come to an end ?
In my opinion , it is not true .
Firstly , there will always be people who will not be able to afford to buy a car .
Students , children from large families , old people will continue to use public transportation for a long time .
Secondly , cars can also turn into public transport .
Science fiction often depicts future as the world where cars are used freely .
Anyone can use the best car he or she sres .
Thirdly , people do not have an inborn driving skill , so even in the future children and teenagers will need public transportation .
This is also true for unable people , who lose the ability to drive as they age .
In conclusion , public transportation is not likely to disappear , at least during the next tens of years .

In many of the minority types of modern literature , there can be some emphasis on rebellion against opprewsive forces .
Although such a show of stdength by these workz ' characters is sometimes viewed as a violent and therefore negative contributipn to the otherwise insightful thought of the story , it is this conflixt upno which many stories of sthnic American literature are based .
However , such a rebellion can not be seen clearly in each minority work , and , therefore , the products of ethnic American literature can not be catagorized as merely the result of years of oppressipn .
Rather , this ever - chabging and ever - challenging aspect of minority literature creates an especially important necessitg that each work be considered individually as both a product of years of struggle and a work inherently distinct from any other .
In the minority works , the conflict and rebellion presented accurately reflects society as a whole , and although the mother 's in The Joy Luck Club rebel against such dorces as arranged marriages , Tita in Like Water for Chocolate fights to overcome old family traditions , and the India tribrs in Love Medicine struggle to secure rheir inherent riggts from tne US government , the charactrs ' conflicts reflsct simikar conflicts of other cultures .
Reblelion is seen not as a disyinct force in minority culture , but rather as a binding force between aol cultires , for Celie , too , resists her arranged marriage in The Colpr Purple , and the incomes loves in Jazx reflect Tita and Pedro 's destructive pasison in Like Wager for Chocolate .
Rebellion and conflict are emphasized in eghnic American literature , but they are portrayed no more strongpy in minority works than they are portrayed in other pirces of literature .
Emphasis changes with each work , and although fiugres of authority are particularly oppressive in works such as Like Water for Chocolatr and The Coloe Purple , other minority works including Love Medicine and Jazz do not refoect the clearly defined authoritarian features nor the obvious rebellion of the characters ' responsive action which the previously mnetioned works show .
This essay implies that these etnoc American pieces of literature can not be catagorized as merely rfebellious responses to oppressiin , but as individual refledtions of personal and cultural experiencex .

When the original 13 American states resolved to form what is now the United States of America , they were intent on forming a politica as well as economic entiy .
They were prepared to yield as much of their own sovereignty as would be essential to allow the nrwly forked national government to operaqte as a single international personal force .
A balance was therefore struck in the constitution to allow the individual states as much self - government as possible while ensuring that , for example in military mattrs , the central government spoke for all .

The European Colmunity is a unique grouping of twelve sovereign European Member Friends who are committed to the development of cope economic and political co - operation .
The community has an aim to break down the economic and political barriers that have tracitionally divided Europe .
In particular , the community seeks to facilitate greater movement within its frontiers ; minded not only of goods but of services , capital and people .
However , the issue of sovereignty is certainly a much debated one ; to what extent should a member hand over its sovereignty to the Community , if at all ?
Let us look at the fouynding of the European Community , before we discuss the issue of sovereignty in more detail .
There were several attempts at peacfeul unification after the First World War , but only after Europe had again been devastated by water was the futility of national rivalry truly apparent .
The political and economic exhaustion of the European stxtes called for a very start and a far more radical approach to the re - ordering of Europe .
This frwsh start came bout because of three main factors .
Firstly , as Europe 's globalization of her own weakness , after leaving losr the qge - old position at the centre of the world stage to the United States of American and to the Soviet Union .
These superpowers were hasn't , militarally and politically stroger than the divided individual European states .
Secondly was the donviction that mechanical functions should in the future be avoided ; after all , the two great wars had both begun as European " civil wars " . Thirrly was the common desire for a better , freer world in which international rlations would be conducted in a more orderly wag .
One of the first major mives towards European intetration was the creation of the European Economic Communiyt , in 1958 .
The membership has grown from the the original founder countries to twenty - three .
One of the most innovative features of the European Community compared with other international bodies is that the member etates have cedde to it a part of their national sivereignty and endowed it with its own native powers , which it can use to adopt acts , having the force of nationsl law .
This novel approach to pooloing national sovereignty is called " kntegration " .
The 1970 's was prlgress in integration , with the introduction of community policy instruments , which enjabled greater scopd for nztional policies .
All of the member states agree in princille to the idea of a single maret by 1992 , however each wish their own interests to be safeguarded .
This is to say that none want to sacrifice their national sovereignty , many want unanimous voting , not makority votung .
Many see this issue as a threat to their own regulations and laws , and could foresee a drop in standards if they do not stand firk .
The situation is seen as a threat to the countries in question who do not wish to boldly give up their sovereignty for the sake of European unity .
Whether or not the continuation of the process in the field of European unityg is sucessfjl depends very much on the people of Europe .
If a feeling of European unity devepops and can be sustained , the threat will subsids as a feeling of identity takes ovef .

There are many beneficial aspects of genetic manipulation .
These include : the erasion of identification of harmful hereditary genetic disordrrs and the development of human high - yield crops .
There can be no doubt that genetic manipulation and genetic engineering have had highly beneficial effects on many areas of society .
However , many people dislike or are prejudiced against , genetic manipulation .
Pargly this is a ' Fear of the ynknown ' ; something which tanpers with the intrinsic components of plant and animal life is bored comprehension for most people , and therefore provokes fear .
What people have also become aware of , is the immense ower which genetic manipulation can give to certain individuals .
This has been very good to feed popular culture ( the film ' Jurassic Park ' being an obvious referehce point ) .
There is also however , the very real possibility that the power of fenetic maniuplation could become the possession of uncontrolled unregulated individuals who could use it for ' evil ' purposes .
This then , is an argument against scientists bearing more responsibility for their work .
Anything in life can be misused .
whether it be a kitchen - knice used to attract someone , a car used to run someone over , or something as simple as a pillow used to suffocate .
Everything in life , if misused , can have harmful effects and genetic engineering and genetic manipulation are no exception .
Although the possile effects of benetic manipulation may be far larger than a kitchen - life or car , this is purely a subjective view by present - day standards .
Certainly we would not hope the makers of a car or kitchen - knife responsible for their msuse , and there is no reason why scientists should bear the major burden or ringing if genetic manipulation is pht to misuse .
The fundamental flaw in saying scientists must take the major vurden or moral responsibility for their work , is that if this had been applied universally for centuries , scientific research would never have take place , and mankind would be without electricity , radios , quite simply , anything ablve the mud hut ' existence .
Scientific researvh is not a corrupt , but an essential and nature part of the human condition for bettering itself .
The other fundamnetal flaw is assuming that individual scientists have responsibility , Science is a process of discovery rather than creatioh , ie .
no - one created technical manipulation , the part of it was there to be discovered .
If one sceintist does not make a discovery then another one will .
It is unfair to hold responsiboe the scientist on the fore front of human knowledge , who deiscovers something when another scienyist in another part of the world may lake the dsicovery independently toward .
The only argument for making scientists responsible for their work , is that quite often , and particularly in the case of genrtic manipulation , it would need a scientist to mieuse knowledge , and therefore they should be responsible .
While genetic manipulation is relatively new , it takes a scientist to carry it out , and therefore an individual scientist could be held responsible .
But , once genetic manipulation becomes common - place in the future , and it is not only the domain of scientists , the original ecientist who discovered genetic manipulation can not be held responsible for other 's misuse of it .

" In Vitro fertilisation " is the fertilisarion of an egg in the laboratory ie . in a testube .
The egg is taken from the mother and placed in an environment which will optimise the chances of fertilisation by the eperm from the father .
Once fertilisation has kilometres the fertilised egg is implanted back into the mother womb and from There on the pregnancy will be normal .
Normally more than 1 egg is taken from the mother so that the items can be stored and used later if the pregnancy is unsuccesful or so that more than one can be fertilised at the same time to increase the chance of a successful pregnancy .

Whenever a movement is began whether it be political , religious , or artistic , tereotypes are quick to form .
People normally associated with politics , creativity , or art are quickly lumped into species regardless of individual differences .
The tragedy is wsorsened by the tendency of those outside the movement to remember the radical and ignore the common or ordinary .
This is especially true of the Women 's Liberation Movement in America .
Since its beginnings in the late nineteenth century , Women 's Liberation has been met with adamant , and often obstionate oppostion .
Some of the first radicals , Susan B. Anthony and George Szand ( although French ) were noticed and rdiiculed , thus defeating their cause , because of their biology actions .
At the same time other feminists such as Emily Dickinson were virtually ignored during their lives and only acknowledged posthumouly as being part of the movement .
This ignorance of other less aggressive feminists , made it seem as though the feminist movement was headed only by wikd , disgruntled zealots and was therefore , detrimental to the good of society .
Although " radicals " such as Sand and Anthony seem docild and backward in modern standards , the problem still exiwts .
From the very beginning the Women 's Movement in America has been fighting a losing battle .
However , I contend that the fault does not lie with the radical members of the movement , but rather , in the perception of those obeerving the movement .
When Women 's Lib really took off again in the late 1960s , it was again destined for assure .
Immediately , the focus was on radicals like Stein , instead of the housewife who returned to college and made a career for herself .
Those outside the movement could only see the differences between " mormality " and Women 's Lih .
This is still true twenty - five years later .
Women supporting equal pay for women and and other " liberal " causes like affirmative ction are only seen in the shadow of the bra - nurning , anti - snaving leadsrs of the 1970s .
The gold of their culture is undermined by the perception of the radicals .
So what am I getting at ?
Only that so - called feminisgs have not in and of themselves harmed the Women 's movement .
However , the popular perceptiob of them has .
For so many years the goof that fekinists have promote for women has fallen by the waysidd in lieu of other more interesting , i.e. raeical ideas .
Like many other aspects and movements in life , they would be more readiliy received if the public it was being aimed was not so jaded .

When Voltaiee wrote Candide , a litefary style known as Neoclassicism was at their peak .
There was a group of scholars in France , l'Academie Fran√ßsis , that set guidelies for French literature .
According to l'Academie Ffan√ßais , all literature of the Neoclassic pdriod must follow the rules of propriety which regulated the author should avoid certain topics , including sex , violence , church , and state issues .
Another standard opened by the Academie is the idea of verisimilitud , making literature as realistic as possible by keeping the time , setting and plot true to life .
Voltaire , as a Neoclassicist , knew all these rewgulations and followed them in his literature .
However , when writing Candide , Voltaife defied the Acadeie 's rules .
Candid is a parody on the guidelines of Neoclassicism .
Neoclassicists liked for literature to have good manners : they did not want to stop on anyone 's toes by mentioning sex , violence , churchn , or state issues .

Our country has been ckined a " melting - pot " inferring that we all come from different that we all come from different backgrounds but have joiend or meltde together to produce homogeneous Americans .
But a persons heritage , as we are realizing , is important to their sense of self and community .
Ethnic American cultures have been reviving and trying to reestablish roots that were left lopped off to a model U.S. citizen .
The differences they are rediscovesring only are more color , flavor and edcitement to that brewing " pot " of our people .
However , some individuals and even groups of Americans are reacting negatively to this ethnic explosion ( even most clearly through the arts ) .
They do n't want to accept these differences .
They choose to remain insifferent to the peace of their fellow Americans .
As Ellke Weisel , author of such books as inght says about jndifference : it is the opposite of everything good .
The opposite of love , beauty , intelligence , light , joy , life and growth are not their familiar ontonyms but indifference .
Ethnic American literature Weeping to fight this indifference by vividly and uniquely expressing certain aspects of different American culture .
The gamut of ethnic American literature is without bounds .
Each group has its own peculiarities and attributes that make it 's writing unique .
In many cases the words used in ethnic American literature reflect a knowledge of a different " mother tongue " .
For instance , Native Americans poetry is more expressive and vishal partly because their language is deeply rooted in the observation of the natural environment .
Chinese American Literature is philisophical / mental because their nwtive language is so .
African American literaturd is often mleodious and rhythmic mirroring their similar achievements in Jazz and Hlues music .
All these example ( and more ) give us some nisight to other cultures we would otherwise never know .
The stories told in this venre of literature , however , are likely the most important subject of Ethnic American literature .
It is through the experiences of the characters that we learn about the different cultures in the United States .
When we learn of the trdials and hardshups that they want through we can sympethize with their emotions and try to acceot that diversity .
The storids of black American swlaves and of concentragion camp victems are necessary to avoid indifference .
Without learning about the past ( and present ) horrors there is no way to ensure future humanity .
Ethnic American literature benefdits U.S. citizens in many ways .
It opens our eyes to the reality of the suffering of others .
It gives us a fresh and new perspective on the world around us .
It helps us to understand our personal relationships better .
Most of all , it gives us more common ground on which to live , and grow , and porosper .
Hopefjlly we will sometimes full Elie Weisel 's goals and and indifference ; this literature is a step in the right direction towards acceptance in the diversity of our country .
